<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представительный.html>представи́тельный</a> (11927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представительный.html>представи́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>representative
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:представительный.html>предста́вительная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выборка.html>вы́борка</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статистика.html>стати́стике</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predstávitelʹnaja</b> výborka (v statístike)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">representative sample</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>imposing, dignified, impressive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:представительный.html>предста́вительная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внешность.html>вне́шность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predstávitelʹnaja</b> vnéšnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">imposing/dignified/impressive appearance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:представительный.html>предста́вительный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predstávitelʹnyj</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dignified/impressive man; man of imposing/dignified appearance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***представительство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представительство.html>представи́тельство</a> (10220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представительство.html>представи́тельство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavítelʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представительство.html>представи́тельства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представительство.html>представи́тельства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представительство.html>представи́тельств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>representation, representative office</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>ста</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ство</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a> (563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to offer</li>
<li>to produce, to show</li>
<li>to introduce, to present</li>
<li>to imagine, to picture, to fancy, to conceive</li>
<li>to perform, to act</li>
<li>to represent, to embody, to depict, to envision, to figure, to realize</li>
<li>to represent, to be</li>
<li>to recommend, to put forward</li></ol>

***представиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представиться.html>предста́виться</a> (3335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представиться.html>предста́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to occur, to present itself; to offer, to arise</li>
<li>to introduce oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́те</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:представиться.html>предста́виться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razrešíte <b>predstávitʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">let me introduce myself</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seem</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pretend (to be), to pass oneself off (as)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больны́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predstavljátʹsja</b> bolʹným</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to feign sickness</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>ста́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ви<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-представ-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***представление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ние</a> (1488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представление.html>представле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>introduction (a means, such as a personal letter, of presenting one person to another)</li>
<li>presentation, submission, introduction</li>
<li>performance, show</li>
<li>idea, notion, conception</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́вший</a> (574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavljávšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представить.html>предста́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to present, to offer</li>
<li>to produce, to show</li>
<li>to introduce, to present</li>
<li>to imagine, to picture, to fancy, to conceive</li>
<li>to perform, to act</li>
<li>to represent, to embody, to depict, to envision, to figure, to realize</li>
<li>to represent, to be</li>
<li>to recommend, to put forward</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a> (2455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstavljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представиться.html>предста́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to occur, to present itself; to offer, to arise</li>
<li>to introduce oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрешить.html>разреши́те</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:представиться.html>предста́виться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razrešíte <b>predstávitʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">let me introduce myself</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seem</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pretend (to be), to pass oneself off (as)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:представляться.html>представля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больны́м</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predstavljátʹsja</b> bolʹným</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to feign sickness</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predstavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***предстоять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предстоять.html>предстоя́ть</a> (1885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предстоять.html>предстоя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predstojátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>no perfective form</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie ahead, to be at hand, to be in the offing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:предстоять.html>предстои́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зима́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam <b>predstoít</b> xolódnaja zimá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We are in for a cold winter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to have to do something in the future
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:предстоять.html>предстои́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туда.html>туда́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>predstoít</b> pojéxatʹ tudá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I shall have to go there</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предупредить.html>предупреди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predupredítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предупреждать.html>предупрежда́ть</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предупредить.html>предупреди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predupredítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предупреждать.html>предупрежда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predupreždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предупредить.html>предупреди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warn, to let know beforehand</li>
<li>to forestall, to anticipate</li>
<li>to avert, to prevent</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотреть.html>предусмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predusmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусматривать.html>предусма́тривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predusmátrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотреть.html>предусмотре́ть</a></b>)

***предусмотреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотреть.html>предусмотре́ть</a> (6707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:усмотреть.html>усмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотреть.html>предусмотре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predusmotrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусматривать.html>предусма́тривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to foresee, to envisage, to anticipate</li>
<li>to provide (for), to stipulate (for)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотрительный.html>предусмотри́тельный</a> (10577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотреть.html>предусмотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predusmotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предусмотрительный.html>предусмотри́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predusmotrítelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)предусмотри́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)предусмотри́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>prudent, precautionary, far-sighted</li></ol>
